[26/03/2024, 21:32:25] Avani Upreti: Certainly! Here's a suggested itinerary for a budget trip to Shimla for 2 days and 2 nights for a group of 4 friends:

**Day 1:**

**Morning:**
1. Start your journey early in the morning from your location to Shimla. You can opt for a bus or train to keep the costs low. Make sure to book tickets in advance to avail any discounts.

**Afternoon:**
2. Arrive in Shimla by afternoon and check into a budget-friendly accommodation. Look for guesthouses or hostels which offer dormitory beds or budget rooms.

**Lunch:**
3. Have lunch at a local eatery or street food vendor to experience the local cuisine without spending too much.

**Afternoon:**
4. Explore Mall Road: Take a stroll along the famous Mall Road. Enjoy the vibrant atmosphere, shop for souvenirs, and taste local snacks like momos and chole bhature.

**Evening:**
5. Visit The Ridge: Enjoy the panoramic views of the surrounding hills and sunset at The Ridge. It's a popular spot for locals and tourists alike.

**Dinner:**
6. Have dinner at one of the affordable restaurants near Mall Road or The Ridge. Look for places serving Himachali dishes like Siddu or Dham for an authentic culinary experience.

**Night:**
7. After dinner, you can either explore the nightlife in Shimla or return to your accommodation for a good night's rest.

**Day 2:**

**Morning:**
1. Breakfast: Start your day with a hearty breakfast at a local cafe or dhaba. Try some parathas or puri bhaji for a filling meal.

**Activity:**
2. Kufri Visit: Take a local bus or shared taxi to Kufri, which is about 13 kilometers from Shimla. Enjoy activities like horse riding, yak riding, or simply soak in the breathtaking views of the snow-capped Himalayan peaks.

**Lunch:**
3. Have lunch at a local restaurant in Kufri, where you can savor some delicious Himachali cuisine.

**Afternoon:**
4. Adventure Park Visit: Visit the Kufri Fun World or the Adventure Resort to indulge in some adventure activities like go-karting, zip-lining, or skiing (seasonal). These places offer budget-friendly adventure options.

**Evening:**
5. Return to Shimla by late afternoon and spend some leisure time exploring the local markets or relaxing at your accommodation.

**Dinner:**
6. For dinner, you can either try a new restaurant or revisit one of your favorite places from the previous day.

**Night:**
7. Spend your last night in Shimla reminiscing about your trip with your friends. You can opt for some stargazing if the weather permits before calling it a night.

**Day 3:**

**Morning:**
1. Check out from your accommodation and head back to your respective destinations, carrying memories of your budget-friendly trip to Shimla.

This itinerary offers a mix of sightseeing, adventure, and local experiences while staying within a budget of 10,000 for a group of 4 friends. Adjustments can be made based on personal preferences and seasonal activities available during your visit.
